 The research wing of the AIIMS Eye Department started investigating the nutritional content of fruits and vegetables to find out the cause of weakness in the retina of the eyes and the results were shocking
 lagbhag teen saal tak chali is study main pataa chalaa ki dakshin bharat main jo fal or subjiyan milti hai, unamem dilli-ensiaar main milane vaale fal or subjiyon ke mukaable paushtik tatwon kii maatra bahut zyada he
 You may be wondering what to do with the study of macula kaphal-vegetables in the retina
 aapkaa bhram ham dur kar dete hai
 The macula is the part of the retina from which it appears very clear but around 50-55 years it starts to weaken
 inamen maujuud cells ko swasth rahane ke liye jis bhojan kii jarurat padati he wo falon or subjiyon main maujuud carotenoids tatv hota he
 Similarly, lycopene present in fruits and vegetables, which is found mainly in tomatoes, beta-carotene, which is found in carrots, also supplies food to the sales of macula
 ames ke research wing ne is baat kii jaanch ke liye kai tarah se kaam shuru kiya
 studydow lasted for three years
 alok kumaar ravi ne bataaya ki shuruyaat main dakshin bharat ke chennai or tamilnadu or aasapaas ke ilaakon se or north india visheshkar ensiaar se 51 subjiyon or 20 falon ke namoonay alag-alag 10 or 12 jagahon se liye gaye the
 The investigation of the nutritional elements present in them took almost three years
 jaanch main paaya gaya ki dilli-ensiaar se milane vaali subjiyon main carotenoids (carotenoids) ke alaava or prakritik tatwon kii maatra kam thi jabaki dakshin bharat main milane vaale falon or subjiyon ke namoonay main isaki maatra bahut zyada thi
 It was also found that the presence of nutritious elements in different fruits and vegetables was also different
 kuch main ye bahut zyada tha jaise ki dilli-ensiaar main bikne vaale kaale angoor main paushtik tatwon kii maatra 14
 70 and its volume in South India was 24
 90 mili
 Similarly its quantity 38 in guava
 40 or dilli main bikne vaale amaruud main paushtik tatwon kii maatra keval 6
 90 ml
 dow
 Alok said that the quality of vegetables and fruits depends on the environment, temperature, method of cultivation, fertilizer etc
 and this study directly indicates that the vegetables grown in North India have low nutritional value for several reasons
 phir bhi south india ke logon main carotenoids kii maatra kamams ne north india se 15 or south india se 13 retina kii jaanch kii to pataa chalaa ki dakshin bharat ke logon ke retina main maujuuda makula main carotenoids kii maatra kam thi jabaki north main jo log the unke makula main ye zyada thi
 Dr
 alok kaa maananaa he ye khanpan par nirbhar karata he
 People in the North consume a lot of vegetables and this is less in South India
 vivaadit or bhadakaau bhaashanon ke liye charchaa main rahane vaale saansad asaduddin ovaisi kaa kahana he ki unki jinna se tulana karnaa galat he kyonki unhone kabhi bhi desh todane kii baat nahin kii
 There is no meaning to the Jinnah statue in AMU
 apane vivaadit bayanon ke liye aksar charchaa main rahane valesaansad asaduddin ovaisine badi bebaaki se muslim raajnneeti or 2019 ke loksabhaa chunaavon par ajtak ke kaarykram 'third degree' main anjana om kashyap, nishanth chaturvedi or ashok singhl ke saath khulkar baat kii

 unhone koi kabhi desh todane kii baat nahin kahi
 He said, 'I always follow the constitution of the country and talk of the country
 'aligarh muslim vishvavidhyalay (eemyu) main jinna kii murti hataane parovaisika kahana he ki beshak vahaan se unki murti hataa di jaae
 They have nothing to do with this
 hamane hameshaa samvidhan kii baat kii he, desh kii baat kii he
 On Muslim politics, Owaisi says that he does not do Muslim politics, he talks about the upliftment of the downtrodden
 unki tarakkee kii baat karte hai
 There is no talk of opening a school, they were always used as a vote bank in the name of upliftment of Muslims
 aaj bhi ve vikaas ke liye taras rahe hai
 They were not allowed to proceed
 unhone kaha, 'main unki aawaaj uthaata hum jo samvidhan main likhaa hua he
 i talk about that
 ' shahid hone vaale surakshabalon kii ginati karne vaale apane vivaadit bayaan par ovaisi kaa kahana he ki agar main shaheedon kii sankhya kii baat karata hum to usamen kisi ko aapatti kya he agar marane waalon main kitne muslim shahid hue hai yah baat uthaai jaati he to isamen kisi ko etraj nahin hona chahie kyonki usase deshbhakti kii bhaavana kaa pataa chalata he ki muslimon main bhi deshbhakti kii bhaavana kam nahin
 On the question of return of Kashmiri Pandits to Jammu and Kashmir, Owaisi said, 'I also wish that Kashmiri Pandits should return home

 About 45 years ago, a movement was started in Uttarakhand, called the Chipko Movement

 chipko andolan kii shuruyaat pradesh ke chamoli jile main gopeshwar naam ke ek sthaan par kii gai thi
 The movement started in 1972 to prevent the indiscriminate and illegal harvesting of forests

 You will no longer be bored of sitting at the New Delhi railway station waiting for the train, as the railway is bringing free wi-fi facilities to this busiest station in India
 yatriyon kii suvidha ke liye stesan par muft vaai-faai dene vaala desh kaa yah pehla stesan hoga
 New Delhi railway station carries around 300 trains and 5 lakh passengers daily
 is stesan ko desh kaa pehla vaai-faai suvidhayukta stesan banaaya jayega, taaki bade antarrashtriya hawaii addon jaisi aadhunik suvidhaayen yahaan mil saken
 "A Mumbai based company has been tasked to make the New Delhi station a wi-fi enabled station," said a senior Railway Ministry official
 unhone kaha ki company kaa chayan nivida ke jariye kiya gaya tha
 wi-fi is a popular networking technique in which high speed wireless Internet and network connections are provided using radio waves
 rail adhikari ne kaha ki ek baar shuru ho jane ke baad stesan ke sabhi 16 platformon par yatri apane laptop yaa mobile phonon ke jariye vaai-faai kii suvidha kaa laabh uthaa sakenge
 The official said that the New Delhi station has been selected on a pilot basis to start this facility costing around 80 lakhs
 tippaniyan He said, this facility is likely to be started in three to four months
 unhone kaha ki company is suvidha ko pahunchane ke liye sabhi ranneetik sthanon par tower lagaaegi
 This facility will also be extended to other stations
 railway haavda rajdhani trainon main pehle hi vaai-faai suvidha uplabdh karvaa rahi he
 There are also plans to replace the information kiosks at the New Delhi station with tablet computers
 adhikari ne kaha, ham yatriyon ke laabh ke liye stesan main kuch jagahon par deevaaron par tablet lagane kii soch rahe hai
 In this tablet, the status of the train, the possible time of arrival and the information required for the passenger will be available
 nai dilli railway stesan par rojaanaa lagbhag teen sau trainon or paanch lakh yatriyon kii awajahi rahati he
 This station will be made the first wi-fi enabled station in the country, so that modern facilities like major international airports can be found here
 rail mantralay ke ek varisht adhikari ne kaha, nai dilli stesan ko vaai-faai suvidhayukta stesan banane ke liye mumbai aadhaarit ek company ko kaam saunpa gaya he
 He said that the company was selected through a tender
 vaai-faai netwarking kii ek charchit takanic he, jisamen radio tarangon ke istemaal se tej gati kaa wireles internet or network conection uplabdh karaayaa jaataa he
 The railway official said that once started, passengers on all 16 platforms of the station will be able to avail the facility of wi-fi through their laptops or mobile phones
 adhikari ne kaha ki lagbhag 80 lakh kii laagat vaali is suvidha kii shuruyaat ke liye nai dilli stesan ko praayogic aadhaar par chunaa gaya he
 The comments unhone kaha, yah suvidha teen se chaar maah main shuru ho jane kii sambhaavna he
 He said that the company would erect towers at all strategic locations to provide this facility
 is suvidha kaa vistaar anya steshnon tak bhi kiya jayega

 nai dilli stesan par soochna dene vaale kiosk ko tablet computaron ke saath badalane kii bhi yojanaayen hai
